[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: untrusted input leads to an uncontrolled [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound network request.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack shows that XML parsing in `PDXFAResource.getDocument` invokes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe JDK’s internal XML parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXerces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which attempts to resolve an external entity[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia HTTP.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The SSRF check is triggered in `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket` when [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Socket.connect` is called.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DomXfaParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplies arbitrary PDF inputs [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining XFA content, but the root behavior arises from PDFBox’s handling of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal XML entities.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Relevant Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **PDXFAResource.getDocument [0m[1;39m([0m[39mApache PDFBox[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** – entry point for loading XFA [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML content.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML parsing stack** – classes under [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.sun.org.apache.xerces.internal.impl.*` and [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`javax.xml.parsers.DocumentBuilderImpl` that handle entity resolution.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network I/O calls** – `HttpURLConnection` and `Socket.connect` invocations [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginated during XML parsing.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Fuzzer harness** – `DomXfaParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` in the user’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode, to understand how untrusted data flows into the XML parser.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic review should trace how untrusted PDF/XFA input leads to external entity[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution and subsequent network connections.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `PDXFAResource.getDocument` method uses a vanilla `DocumentBuilderFactory`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout disabling external entity resolution or DTD loading. As a result, when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing untrusted XFA XML, the JDK’s XML parser can follow external entity [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., system identifiers pointing to `[0m[4;94mhttp://jazze.com:80`[0m[4;94m)[0m[4;94m,[0m[39m triggering[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Harden the XML parser configuration in `PDXFAResource.getDocument` to prevent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many external network access or DTD/entity resolution. This is a standard XXE/SSRF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigation: disable external-general-entities, external-parameter-entities, DTD [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading, and enable secure processing. Additionally, install a no‐op [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`EntityResolver` to catch any residual entity-resolution attempts.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify `PDXFAResource.getDocument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpdfbox/src/main/java/org/apache/pdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/PDXFAResource.java[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m:[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after obtaining the factory [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mDocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, apply the following:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • `[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl"[0m[39m, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entities"[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/nonvalidating/load-external-dtd[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • `[0m[1;35mfactory.setXIncludeAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • `[0m[1;35mfactory.setExpandEntityReferences[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After creating the `DocumentBuilder`, set a benign `EntityResolver`:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mbuilder.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Preserve the existing `[0m[1;35m.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mByteArrayInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mthis.getBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Rationale[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - These features collectively disable any resolution of external [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTDs/entities, block DOCTYPE declarations entirely, and enforce secure-processing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimits. The custom `EntityResolver` ensures that if the parser still attempts to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve an entity, it will receive an empty stream rather than opening network [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This approach does not alter the public API of `PDXFAResource`: callers [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill receive a standard DOM `Document`. Any inline XFA XML will continue to parse [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas before, as in-memory entity references [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are still expanded to empty or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault content rather than fetching over HTTP.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Maintaining Existing Functionality[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Inline content [0m[1;39m([0m[39melements, attributes, text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unaffected. XFA forms [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat rely solely on embedded XML will continue to function. Only external [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTD/entity resolution is suppressed, which is acceptable for secure processing.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No changes are made to the fuzzer harness, external libraries, or tests, so[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and fuzz targets remain valid.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If legitimate XFA forms rely on external DTDs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrare in PDF/XFA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, those [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures will no longer load. However, loading remote DTDs is a known security risk[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand is discouraged.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should a use-case arise where external entities are legitimately required, a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontrolled, whitelist-based entity resolver can be added later. For now, the strict[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault prevents SSRF without breaking typical inline XFA parsing.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OWASP XXE Prevention: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [4;94mhttps://cheatsheetseries.owasp.org/cheatsheets/XML_External_Entity_Prevention_Cheat[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [4;94m_Sheet.html[0m[39m  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar hardening patterns exist in other PDFBox parsers, e.g., `PDFParser`’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DocumentBuilderFactory` usage in `COSParser`.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. No further harness or test modifications are needed. The patch is contained [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely within `PDXFAResource.getDocument`. [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
